S2.3.1 CD8 + T Cells ŌåÆ B Cells 

Across 845 donors, MR-CCC evaluated 42 ligandŌĆōreceptorŌĆōpathway triplets for the CD8 + Tcell (sender) to B cell (receiver) direction and identified seven high-confidence causal commu-nication signals with PIP exceeding 0.5 (Figures S25ŌĆōS27). The seven triplets span two path-way classes: six Adhesion by ICAM pairs ( ICAM2 ŌĆōITGAL , PIP = 0 .861; ICAM1 ŌĆōITGAX ,PIP = 0 .755; ICAM1 ŌĆōITGAL , PIP = 0 .738; ICAM2 ŌĆōITGB2 , PIP = 0 .712; ICAM1 ŌĆō

ITGAM , PIP = 0 .676; ICAM1 ŌĆōITGB2 , PIP = 0 .556) and one Signaling by Interleukin triplet ( IL23A ŌĆōIL12RB1 , PIP = 0 .800). 

Adhesion by ICAM signals. The six discovered ICAMŌĆōintegrin triplets again implicate the CD8 + T cellŌĆōB cell adhesive interface, where ICAM family members on T cells engage 

╬▓2 integrins on B cells 20,23 . In contrast to the CD4 + T cells ŌåÆ B cells direction ŌĆöwhere the six ICAM pairs produced a heterogeneous fan including both strongly stimulatory and strongly suppressive curvesŌĆöthe CD8 + T cell ICAM contacts are predominantly suppressive at physiological receptor expression levels, consistent with the cytotoxic rather than helper function of CD8 + T cells at the T cellŌĆōB cell interface. All six curves are visible in the Adhesion by ICAM panel (Figure S27). The top-ranked ICAM pair, ICAM2 ŌĆōITGAL (PIP = 0 .861, ╦å╬▓X = 0 .165, ╦å╬▓XZ = ŌłÆ3.98), has a near-zero main effect and a large negative interaction, producing a curve that crosses zero at only ZŌłŚ Ōēł +0 .04 standard deviations above the mean ITGAL levelŌĆöessentially at the population mean. For B cells expressing LFA-1 above this threshold, which encompasses the vast majority of the observed population, CD8 + T cell ICAM2 engagement exerts a steeply increasing suppression of Adhesion pathway activity, with the effect growing strongly negative at high LFA-1 densities. This contrasts markedly with the CD4 + T cells ŌåÆ B cells direction, where ICAM2 ŌĆōITGAL had a large positive interaction ( ╦å╬▓XZ = 2 .59), yielding the opposite receptor-modulated outcome despite the same ligandŌĆōreceptor pair. Of the four discovered ICAM1 ŌĆōintegrin pairs, ICAM1 ŌĆōITGAX (PIP = 0 .755, ╦å╬▓X =

ŌłÆ0.758, ╦å╬▓XZ = ŌłÆ2.50) and ICAM1 ŌĆōITGAL (PIP = 0 .738, ╦å╬▓X = ŌłÆ0.986, ╦å╬▓XZ = 0 .927) 46 show the largest coefficient magnitudes. ICAM1 ŌĆōITGAX crosses zero at approximately 0.30 standard deviations below the mean ITGAX level, placing essentially the full observed CD11c-expressing B cell population in the suppressive regime, with the suppression inten-sifying steeply at high receptor density. ICAM1 ŌĆōITGAL has a negative main effect and a partially positive interaction, crossing zero at approximately +1 .06 standard deviations above the mean ITGAL level; because this threshold is well above the population mean, the majority of B cells experience a net suppressive effect of CD8 + T cell ICAM1 engage-ment through LFA-1. ICAM1 ŌĆōITGAM (PIP = 0 .676, ╦å╬▓X = ŌłÆ0.902, ╦å╬▓XZ = ŌłÆ0.782) and 

ICAM1 ŌĆōITGB2 (PIP = 0 .556, ╦å╬▓X = ŌłÆ0.690, ╦å╬▓XZ = ŌłÆ0.893) are both monotonically sup-pressive with zero crossings at approximately 1 .15 and 0 .77 standard deviations below the mean receptor expression level, respectively, placing the entire observed population of B cells in the suppressive regime for both pairs. The exception within the ICAM discoveries is ICAM2 ŌĆōITGB2 (PIP = 0 .712, ╦å╬▓X = 0 .195, ╦å╬▓XZ = 1 .61): both the main effect and the interaction are positive, yielding a monotonically increasing curve that crosses zero approximately 0 .12 standard deviations below the mean 

ITGB2 level and rises steeply with ╬▓2 density. The divergence between ICAM2 ŌĆōITGAL 

(strongly suppressive via LFA-1) and ICAM2 ŌĆōITGB2 (monotonically activating via the ╬▓2

chain alone) indicates that the identity of the integrin chain engaged by CD8 + T cell ICAM2 governs the sign of the downstream B cell Adhesion pathway response. 

Interleukin signal. The IL23A ŌĆōIL12RB1 triplet (PIP = 0 .800, ╦å╬▓X = 0 .904, ╦å╬▓XZ = ŌłÆ3.17) recapitulates the same ligandŌĆōreceptorŌĆōpathway axis discovered in the CD4 + T cells ŌåÆ Bcells direction (PIP = 0 .798), but with a strikingly opposite interaction sign. In the CD4 +

sender direction, the interaction was large and positive ( ╦å╬▓XZ = 3 .16), producing a monoton-ically and steeply stimulatory curve through IL-12R ╬▓1; here, the interaction is equally large but negative ( ╦å╬▓XZ = ŌłÆ3.17), producing a sign-reversing curve that crosses zero at approxi-mately 0 .29 standard deviations above the mean IL12RB1 level and descends steeply there-after. B cells with below-average IL-12R ╬▓1 expression therefore experience a strong stimu-latory response to CD8 + T cell IL-23A production, while those with above-average receptor expression undergo progressively stronger suppression. The exact inversion of the interac-47 tion term between the CD4 + and CD8 + sender directions for the same tripletŌĆö ╦å╬▓XZ Ōēł +3 .16 versus ╦å╬▓XZ Ōēł ŌłÆ 3.17ŌĆöis a striking example of sender-cell-specific modulation of the same ligandŌĆōreceptorŌĆōpathway axis, underscoring the capacity of MR-CCC to detect qualitatively different causal communication patterns from different sender cell populations 25 .

Low-PIP pairs. WNT7A ŌĆōFZD3 (PIP = 0 .458) was the highest-ranking non-discovered triplet, a notable near-miss for which no established biological basis exists for CD8 + T cell WNT signaling to B cells 13 . IFNG ŌĆōIFNGR1 (PIP = 0 .087) and IFNG ŌĆōIFNGR2 (PIP = 0 .074) both received near-zero PIPs despite CD8 + cytotoxic T cells being a major physio-logical source of IFN-╬│ 10 . The low PIPs here likely reflect that IFN-╬│-driven B cell Interferon pathway activity is not well-explained by direct CD8 + T cell cis-eQTL variation for IFNG 

at the population level in this cohort, or that the target pathway genes in B cells are insuf-ficiently variable to detect this signal. IL15 ŌĆōIL15RA (PIP = 0 .094) and IL15 ŌĆōIL2RB (PIP = 0 .101) received near-zero support, consistent with B cells not being primary targets of IL-15-mediated homeostatic signaling 4.48 0.74 0.56 0.68 0.76 0.86 0.71 0.80 

PIP = 0.5

ReceptorŌłÆmodulated ligand effects: CD8 + T cells ŌłÆ> B cells (MRŌłÆCCC) Figure S27: Receptor-modulated effect curves ( ╦å╬▓X + ╦å╬▓XZ ┬Ę Z/ SD( Z)) for the CD8 +

In the Adhesion by ICAM panel, six curves form a predomi-nantly downward-sloping fan: ICAM2 ŌĆōITGAL and ICAM1 ŌĆōITGAX descend most steeply to strongly negative values at high receptor expression, while ICAM1 ŌĆōITGAM and ICAM1 ŌĆō

In the Signaling by Interleukin panel, the IL23A ŌĆōIL12RB1 curve starts at a strongly positive value at low receptor expression and descends steeply, crossing zero near +0 .29 standard deviations above the mean and reaching strongly negative values at high IL-12R ╬▓1 density. 51 S2.3.2 CD8 + T Cells ŌåÆ CD4 + T Cells 

Across 882 donors, MR-CCC evaluated 42 ligandŌĆōreceptorŌĆōpathway triplets for the CD8 + Tcell (sender) to CD4 + T cell (receiver) direction. No triplet reached the PIP > 0.5 discovery threshold: the highest-ranking pair, CXCL8 ŌĆōCXCR2 , achieved a PIP of only 0.367, and the distribution of PIPs was compressed below 0.4 across all 42 triplets (Figures S28ŌĆōS29). Because no triplet exceeded the PIP > 0.5 threshold, no receptor-modulated effect curves are displayed for this direction. This null result is consistent with the biological asymmetry of the CD8 +ŌĆōCD4 + T cell axis: CD8 + cytotoxic T cells are primarily effectors of target-cell killing and cytokine-mediated immune regulation, and do not function as major ligand-expressing senders of pathway-activating signals to CD4 + T cells in the context of peripheral blood homeostasis. The absence of high-PIP discoveries here, alongside the substantial number of discoveries identified for the reverse direction (CD4 + T cells ŌåÆ CD8 + T cells; three triplets, PIP up to 0.668), underscores the directional specificity of MR-CCC and the biological asymmetry of helper versus cytotoxic T cell communication in peripheral blood. Among the highest-ranking sub-threshold triplets, CXCL8 ŌĆōCXCR2 (PIP = 0 .367, ╦å╬▓X =

ŌłÆ0.145, ╦å╬▓XZ = 0 .795) reflects the capacity of activated CD8 + T cells to produce CXCL8 (IL-8), which can engage CXCR2 on CD4 + T cells; however, CXCR2 expression on CD4 + Tcells is limited and variable in peripheral blood, likely attenuating the population-level causal signal below the discovery threshold. IL15 ŌĆōIL2RB (PIP = 0 .334, ╦å╬▓X = 0 .196, ╦å╬▓XZ = 0 .557) and IL15 ŌĆōIL15RA (PIP = 0 .235, ╦å╬▓X = 0 .163, ╦å╬▓XZ = 0 .054) both represent the potential for CD8 + T cells to contribute to IL-15-mediated signaling to CD4 + T cells through the shared IL-2R ╬▓ chain and the high-affinity IL-15R ╬▒ chain 4,14 ; the sub-threshold PIPs suggest this IL-15 axis from CD8 + T cells to CD4 + T cells is insufficiently consistent at the popu-lation level compared with the B cell sender direction, where both chains were discovered. 

SEMA4A ŌĆōPLXND1 (PIP = 0 .320) and SEMA4C ŌĆōPLXNB2 (PIP = 0 .258) represent the two highest-ranking Semaphorin pathway near-misses, consistent with semaphorin expres-sion on activated CD8 + T cells but insufficient to drive a detectable causal communication effect on CD4 + T cell Semaphorin pathway activity 27 . IFNG ŌĆōIFNGR1 (PIP = 0 .032) and 

IFNG ŌĆōIFNGR2 (PIP = 0 .030) received near-zero support despite CD8 + cytotoxic T cells 52 being a major physiological source of IFN-╬│; the very low PIPs indicate that CD8 + T cell-derived IFN-╬│ does not exert a detectable causal effect on CD4 + T cell Interferon pathway activity at the population level in this cohort, in contrast to the CD4 + T cells ŌåÆ NK cells direction where IFNG ŌĆōIFNGR2 was discovered 10,28 .PIP = 0.5

S2.3.3 CD8 + T Cells ŌåÆ NK Cells 

Across 830 donors, MR-CCC evaluated 42 ligandŌĆōreceptorŌĆōpathway triplets for the CD8 +

T cell (sender) to NK cell (receiver) direction and identified one high-confidence causal communication signal with PIP exceeding 0.5: ICAM1 ŌĆōITGAX within the Adhesion by ICAM pathway (PIP = 0 .642) (Figures S30ŌĆōS32). The sole discovery, ICAM1 ŌĆōITGAX (PIP = 0 .642), implicates CD8 + T cell intercel-lular adhesion molecule 1 ( ICAM1 ) as a causal regulator of NK cell Adhesion pathway activity through the integrin ╬▒X chain (CD11c, encoded by ITGAX ), which pairs with ╬▓2

54 (CD18) to form complement receptor 4 (CR4, p150,95) expressed on mature NK cells and myeloid cells 20,21 . The near-zero main effect ( ╦å╬▓X = 0 .024) and large negative interaction ( ╦å╬▓XZ = ŌłÆ2.25) produce a curve that crosses zero approximately 0 .01 standard deviations above the mean ITGAX levelŌĆöessentially at the population mean. The causal signal is therefore almost entirely interaction-driven: NK cells expressing ITGAX at or above the population mean experience a steeply increasing suppression of Adhesion pathway activity upon CD8 + T cell ICAM1 contact, while those with below-mean CD11c expression are ef-fectively unaffected. This receptor-gated suppressive pattern mirrors the ICAM1 ŌĆōITGAX 

discovery in the B cells ŌåÆ Monocytes direction (PIP = 0 .562, ╦å╬▓XZ = ŌłÆ2.04), where CD11c-high monocytes similarly experienced contact-mediated suppression via the same integrin 

╬▒X axis, suggesting that CD11c expression level is a general gate for ICAM1-mediated sup-pressive adhesion contacts across multiple receiver cell types. Notably, several triplets narrowly missed the discovery threshold. CLEC2B ŌĆōKLRF1 

(PIP = 0 .498) was the highest-ranking sub-threshold triplet, with a PIP essentially at the discovery boundary. This pair implicates AICL (activation-induced C-type lectin, encoded by CLEC2B ) on CD8 + T cells as a ligand for the activating NK receptor NKp80 (encoded by KLRF1 ), an axis established to mediate mutual cytotoxic activation between NK cells and myeloid cells, and expressed on activated T cells 30 . The moderately negative main effect ( ╦å╬▓X = ŌłÆ0.097) and negative interaction ( ╦å╬▓XZ = ŌłÆ0.495) produce a predominantly suppres-sive curve for NK cells expressing KLRF1 above approximately 0 .20 standard deviations below the mean, encompassing the majority of the observed population. The PTGES3 ŌĆō

PTGER2 triplet (PIP = 0 .423) again represents the PGE 2ŌĆōEP2 axis on NK cells, which was discovered from B cell (PIP = 0 .556) and CD4 + T cell (PIP = 0 .625) senders but re-mains sub-threshold from the CD8 + sender, suggesting that CD8 + T cells are less dominant prostaglandin producers than B cells or CD4 + T cells in this cohort 18 . ICAM1 ŌĆōITGAM (PIP = 0 .375) and ICAM2 ŌĆōITGAL (PIP = 0 .369) were notable Adhesion by ICAM near-misses, both showing near-zero main effects with moderate negative interactions ( ╦å╬▓XZ = ŌłÆ1.14 and 

ŌłÆ0.359, respectively), indicating receptor-density-gated suppressive contacts that fell below the discovery threshold. PTGES3 ŌĆōPTGER4 (PIP = 0 .367) provided parallel evidence for 55 a sub-threshold PGE 2ŌĆōEP4 axis through a distinct prostaglandin receptor. IFNG ŌĆōIFNGR2 

(PIP = 0 .209) and IFNG ŌĆōIFNGR1 (PIP = 0 .137) were both sub-threshold; the contrast with the CD4 + T cells ŌåÆ NK cells direction, where IFNG ŌĆōIFNGR2 was discovered (PIP = 0 .542), likely reflects greater heterogeneity in IFN-╬│ production across CD8 + T cell states at the population level compared with the more coordinated Th1-driven IFN-╬│ output of CD4 + T cells 10,28 .56 0.64 

PIP = 0.5

Across 678 donors, MR-CCC evaluated 42 ligandŌĆōreceptorŌĆōpathway triplets for the CD8 +

T cell (sender) to Monocyte (receiver) direction and identified two high-confidence causal communication signals with PIP exceeding 0.5, both involving the cytokine IL18 paired with components of its heterodimeric receptor complex (Figures S33ŌĆōS35). 

Signaling by Interleukin. IL18 ŌĆōIL18R1 attained PIP = 0 .82 with ╦å╬▓X = 0 .515 and ╦å╬▓XZ = 1 .63, indicating that the positive main effect of IL18 on monocyte Interleukin pathway activity is amplified as monocyte IL18R1 levels rise. The sign-reversal threshold ZŌłŚ =

ŌłÆ ╦å╬▓X / ╦å╬▓XZ Ōēł ŌłÆ 0.32 SD lies well below the population mean, so the causal effect is positive across essentially the entire monocyte population and increases monotonically with receptor abundanceŌĆöconsistent with a feed-forward architecture in which IL-18-responsive monocytes upregulate the very receptor subunit ( IL18R1 , the ligand-binding ╬▒ chain) that mediates the response 32 .

IL18 ŌĆōIL18RAP attained PIP = 0 .85 with ╦å╬▓X = 0 .483 and ╦å╬▓XZ = ŌłÆ1.87. Here the receptor covariate is IL18RAP , the signal-transducing ╬▓ (accessory-protein) chain of the same heterodimer 33 . The negative ╦å╬▓XZ means that monocytes expressing high levels of the accessory chain show an attenuated ŌĆöand, above the sign-reversal threshold ZŌłŚ Ōēł +0 .26 SD, 

reversed ŌĆöcausal effect of IL18 . Together with the IL18 ŌĆōIL18R1 result, this suggests that the two receptor chains are not simply co-regulated: monocytes with relatively abundant ╬▒

chain are sensitized to IL-18, whereas monocytes with relatively abundant ╬▓ accessory chain may exhibit saturated or downregulated signaling, and can even show a negative responseŌĆö potentially through receptor desensitization or negative-feedback pathways downstream of IL-18R 32,33 .The most notable sub-threshold triplets were ICAM3 ŌĆōITGB2 (PIP = 0 .43), IFNG ŌĆō

IFNGR2 (PIP = 0 .40), and IFNG ŌĆōIFNGR1 (PIP = 0 .39). The IFN-╬│ pairs are biologically noteworthy: CD8 + T cells are a principal source of IFN-╬│ and monocytes express both receptor chains at high levels, yet neither triplet crossed the discovery threshold here, in contrast to the CD4 + T cells ŌåÆ NK cells direction where IFNG ŌĆōIFNGR2 was robustly discovered (PIP = 0 .542). This likely reflects greater donor-to-donor variability in CD8 +

60 IFN-╬│ secretion relative to CD4 + Th1 cells in this cohort, or a more complex multivariate architecture for CD8-mediated monocyte activation that is not fully captured by a single ligandŌĆōreceptor pair 28 .0.82 0.85 

PIP = 0.5

chains of the IL-18 receptor heterodimer. 63 S2.4 NK Cells as Sender 

S2.4.1 NK Cells ŌåÆ B Cells 

Across 818 donors, MR-CCC evaluated 42 ligandŌĆōreceptorŌĆōpathway triplets for the NK cell (sender) to B cell (receiver) direction and identified six high-confidence causal communication signals with PIP exceeding 0.5: four Adhesion by ICAM pairs ( ICAM1 ŌĆōITGAL , PIP = 0.782; ICAM2 ŌĆōITGAL , PIP = 0 .738; ICAM1 ŌĆōITGAM , PIP = 0 .603; ICAM1 ŌĆōITGAX ,PIP = 0 .507), one Signaling by GABA triplet ( SLC6A6 ŌĆōGABBR1 , PIP = 0 .618), and one Signaling by Prostaglandin triplet ( PTGES3 ŌĆōPTGER2 , PIP = 0 .544) (Figures S36ŌĆōS38). 

Adhesion by ICAM signals. The four discovered ICAMŌĆōintegrin triplets collectively implicate NK cell adhesion molecule contacts as causal regulators of B cell Adhesion pathway activity, paralleling the multi-ICAM discovery pattern observed from CD4 + and CD8 + T cell senders 20,23 . The dominant pair, ICAM1 ŌĆōITGAL (PIP = 0 .782, ╦å╬▓X = 0 .961, ╦å╬▓XZ = ŌłÆ2.13), has a large positive main effect and a negative interaction, yielding a sign-reversing curve that crosses zero approximately 0 .45 standard deviations above the mean ITGAL level. B cells expressing LFA-1 below this threshold experience a net stimulatory response to NK cell ICAM-1 engagement; those with above-average LFA-1 density transition to a progressively suppressive effect. This receptor-gated switch mirrors the same ICAM1 ŌĆōITGAL pattern observed from CD4 + and CD8 + T cell senders, indicating that LFA-1 density on B cells is a general determinant of the direction of ICAM-1-mediated adhesion signals regardless of the lymphocyte sender type. In contrast, ICAM2 ŌĆōITGAL (PIP = 0 .738, ╦å╬▓X = ŌłÆ0.046, ╦å╬▓XZ = 5 .29) has a near-zero main effect and an unusually large positive interaction, placing the zero crossing at only Ōēł 0.01 standard deviations above the meanŌĆöessentially at the population mean. The causal signal is therefore almost entirely interaction-driven: B cells expressing ITGAL at or above the mean experience a steeply amplified positive response to NK cell ICAM2, while those below the mean are effectively unaffected. The opposing interaction signs for ICAM1 ŌĆō

ITGAL ( ╦å╬▓XZ = ŌłÆ2.13) and ICAM2 ŌĆōITGAL ( ╦å╬▓XZ = 5 .29) through the same LFA-1 receptor recapitulate the divergent ICAM1 versus ICAM2 pattern seen from CD4 + and CD8 + senders: 64 at high LFA-1 densities, NK cell ICAM1 contact is suppressive while NK cell ICAM2 contact is strongly stimulatory. 

ICAM1 ŌĆōITGAM (PIP = 0 .603, ╦å╬▓X = 0 .786, ╦å╬▓XZ = ŌłÆ3.08) follows the same receptor-gated suppressive pattern as ICAM1 ŌĆōITGAL , with the zero crossing at approximately 0 .26 standard deviations above the mean ITGAM level; B cells expressing the Mac-1 ╬▒ chain (CD11b) above this threshold experience progressively stronger suppression of Adhesion pathway activity upon NK cell ICAM-1 contact 21 .The fourth ICAM discovery, ICAM1 ŌĆōITGAX (PIP = 0 .507, ╦å╬▓X = 0 .530, ╦å╬▓XZ = 0 .056), is qualitatively distinct from the other three: the interaction term is negligibly small and positive, placing the zero crossing at approximately ŌłÆ9.4 standard deviations below the meanŌĆöfar outside the observed data range. This triplet therefore represents a near-purely main-effect discovery: NK cell ICAM-1 exerts a uniformly positive causal effect on the Adhesion pathway activity of B cells expressing ITGAX (CD11c), independent of receptor expression level. CD11c + B cells are a recognized subset (including age-associated B cells and activated B cell subpopulations) with an altered adhesion receptor profile 20 , and the flat, uniformly positive curve suggests that NK cell ICAM-1 constitutively engages this subset irrespective of CD11c density. 

Signaling by GABA. SLC6A6 ŌĆōGABBR1 (PIP = 0 .618, ╦å╬▓X = ŌłÆ0.042, ╦å╬▓XZ = ŌłÆ3.32) implicates NK cell taurine and ╬▓-alanine transporter activity ( SLC6A6 ) as a causal sup-pressor of B cell GABA-B receptor-mediated pathway activity. With a near-zero main effect and a large negative interaction, the zero crossing lies essentially at the population-mean 

GABBR1 expression level ( ZŌłŚ Ōēł ŌłÆ 0.013 SD): B cells expressing GABBR1 at or above the mean experience a steeply increasing suppression of GABA signaling pathway activity as NK cell taurine-transport activity rises. Taurine, the primary substrate of SLC6A6, is a known partial agonist of GABA B receptors and provides a mechanistic link between NK cell amino-acid transport and GABA-B receptor signaling in neighboring cells 8,9 . This triplet was also discovered in the B cells ŌåÆ CD4 + T cells direction (PIP = 0 .54), but there the interaction was large and positive ( ╦å╬▓XZ = 2 .01), yielding a stimulatory rather than sup-pressive receptor-amplified effect. The sign reversal of the GABBR1 interaction between 65 receiver cell typesŌĆöstimulatory for CD4 + T cells, suppressive for B cellsŌĆöillustrates how the same ligandŌĆōreceptor axis can mediate qualitatively different outcomes depending on the downstream signaling environment of the recipient cell. 

Signaling by Prostaglandin. PTGES3 ŌĆōPTGER2 (PIP = 0 .544, ╦å╬▓X = 0 .438, ╦å╬▓XZ =

ŌłÆ1.97) links NK cell prostaglandin E synthase 3 ( PTGES3 ) to the EP2 prostaglandin recep-tor (encoded by PTGER2 ) on B cells. The positive main effect and negative interaction pro-duce a sign-reversing curve that crosses zero approximately 0 .22 standard deviations above the mean PTGER2 level: B cells with low EP2 expression experience a net stimulatory response to NK cell PGE 2 output, while those above the threshold undergo progressively stronger suppression of Prostaglandin pathway activity 18 . This PGE 2ŌĆōEP2 axis has now been discovered across multiple sender types targeting NK cells (B cell sender, PIP = 0 .556; CD4 + T cell sender, PIP = 0 .625), and here NK cells themselves appear as a PGE 2 sender, now acting on B cells as receiver. The recurrence of PTGES3 ŌĆōPTGER2 across directions involving NK cellsŌĆöboth as receiver and as senderŌĆösuggests that PGE 2ŌĆōEP2 signaling is a constitutively active immunomodulatory axis in the NK cell niche of peripheral blood. Several triplets narrowly missed the discovery threshold. ICAM1 ŌĆōITGB2 (PIP = 0 .480) was the highest-ranking sub-threshold triplet, with a PIP at the discovery boundary; the modest positive main effect ( ╦å╬▓X = 0 .568) and positive interaction ( ╦å╬▓XZ = 1 .65) produce a monotonically increasing curve, and its near-discovery suggests the ╬▓2 chain axis from NK cells is borderline consistent at the population level. IL6 ŌĆōIL6ST (PIP = 0 .434) was a notable near-miss; the IL-6/gp130 axis was discovered from both B cell (PIP = 0 .554) and CD4 + T cell (not discovered) senders, and its sub-threshold PIP here suggests NK cells are not a dominant population-level source of IL-6 in peripheral blood. PTGES3 ŌĆōPTGER4 

(PIP = 0 .416) was the second prostaglandin near-miss, indicating that the EP4 receptor axis on B cells is weaker than EP2 in this NK sender direction. 

IFNG ŌĆōIFNGR1 (PIP = 0 .046) and IFNG ŌĆōIFNGR2 (PIP = 0 .045) both received near-zero support despite NK cells being a major physiological source of IFN-╬│ 10 . The very low PIPs likely reflect that B cells express IFN-╬│ receptors at comparatively low levels relative to myeloid and T cell populations in peripheral blood, limiting the causal footprint of NK 66 cell-derived IFN-╬│ on B cell Interferon pathway activity at the population level. 0.78 0.60 0.51 0.74 0.62 0.54

Across 850 donors, MR-CCC evaluated 42 ligandŌĆōreceptorŌĆōpathway triplets for the NK cell (sender) to CD4 + T cell (receiver) direction and identified one high-confidence causal communication signal with PIP exceeding 0.5: ICAM1 ŌĆōITGAL within the Adhesion by ICAM pathway (PIP = 0 .54) (Figures S39ŌĆōS41). The sole discovery, ICAM1 ŌĆōITGAL (PIP = 0 .54, ╦å╬▓X = ŌłÆ0.064, ╦å╬▓XZ = ŌłÆ0.910), impli-cates NK cell intercellular adhesion molecule 1 ( ICAM1 ) as a causal suppressor of CD4 +

T cell Adhesion pathway activity through LFA-1 (encoded by ITGAL )20,23 . The near-zero main effect and moderate negative interaction place the zero crossing at approximately 0 .07 standard deviations below the mean ITGAL levelŌĆöessentially at the population mean. The signal is therefore almost entirely interaction-driven: CD4 + T cells expressing LFA-1 at or above the population mean experience a progressively stronger suppression of Adhesion pathway activity upon NK cell ICAM-1 engagement, while those with the lowest LFA-1 expression are effectively unaffected. This suppressive NKŌĆōCD4 contact through ICAM-1ŌĆō LFA-1 is consistent with the established capacity of NK cells to exert regulatory restraint on T cell activation through direct cellŌĆōcell adhesion, limiting excessive CD4 + T cell re-sponses in an LFA-1 density-dependent manner 20,23 . The ICAM1 ŌĆōITGAL triplet was also discovered in the NK cells ŌåÆ B cells direction (PIP = 0 .782, ╦å╬▓XZ = ŌłÆ2.13), where the same suppressive interaction sign was observed; the considerably smaller interaction magnitude here ( ╦å╬▓XZ = ŌłÆ0.910 versus ŌłÆ2.13) suggests that NK cell ICAM-1 contact is a less potent suppressor of Adhesion pathway activity in CD4 + T cells than in B cells at the population level. Two triplets narrowly missed the discovery threshold and merit specific attention. ICAM1 ŌĆō

ITGAX (PIP = 0 .491, ╦å╬▓X = ŌłÆ0.154, ╦å╬▓XZ = 1 .03) was the highest-ranking sub-threshold triplet; the negative main effect and positive interaction produce a sign-reversing curve that crosses zero approximately 0 .15 standard deviations above the mean ITGAX level, with CD4 + T cells expressing high CD11c showing a net positive Adhesion pathway response to NK cell ICAM-1 contact. ICAM4 ŌĆōITGAL (PIP = 0 .487, ╦å╬▓X = ŌłÆ0.156, ╦å╬▓XZ = ŌłÆ4.20) was the second borderline near-miss; despite failing to clear the threshold, it carries the largest 70 interaction magnitude of any triplet in this direction and a zero crossing only 0 .037 standard deviations below the mean, placing essentially the entire CD4 + T cell population in a regime of steeply increasing suppression of Adhesion pathway activity as NK cell ICAM4 produc-tion rises. The co-occurrence of near-misses for both ICAM1 ŌĆōITGAX (PIP = 0 .491) and 

ICAM4 ŌĆōITGAL (PIP = 0 .487) just below the discovery boundary, alongside the confirmed 

ICAM1 ŌĆōITGAL discovery, indicates that the NKŌĆōCD4 adhesion axis involves multiple par-tially consistent ICAMŌĆōintegrin contacts at the population level that collectively fall near the discovery threshold. Among other sub-threshold triplets, SEMA4A ŌĆōPLXND1 (PIP = 0 .364) represents the highest-ranking Semaphorin pathway near-miss; SEMA4C ŌĆōPLXNB2 (PIP = 0 .261) provides parallel evidence for sub-threshold NK semaphorin signaling to CD4 + T cells, consistent with the established role of semaphorin-plexin contacts in lymphocyte co-stimulation and cytoskeletal regulation 27,34 . LIPA ŌĆōRORA (PIP = 0 .357) was a notable Cholesterol pathway near-miss; this triplet was discovered from B cell senders in the B cells ŌåÆ CD4 + T cells direction (PIP = 0 .686), but here the PIP falls considerably below threshold, consistent with NK cells having lower lysosomal lipid-catabolic activity than B cells 7. AKR1C3 ŌĆō

PTGDR (PIP = 0 .323) indicates a borderline prostaglandin D 2ŌĆōDP receptor axis that does not achieve discovery strength in this direction. 

IFNG ŌĆōIFNGR1 (PIP = 0 .041) and IFNG ŌĆōIFNGR2 (PIP = 0 .049) both received near-zero support despite NK cells being a major physiological source of IFN-╬│ 10,28 . The low PIPs here likely reflect that CD4 + T cell Interferon pathway activity is not well-explained by NK cell cis-eQTL variation for IFNG at the population level, or that the IFN-╬│ signal from NK cells to CD4 + T cells is overshadowed by autocrine or CD4 + Th1-derived IFN-╬│

signaling within the CD4 + compartment itself. SLC6A6 ŌĆōGABBR1 (PIP = 0 .034) received a near-zero PIP despite being discovered in the NK cells ŌåÆ B cells direction (PIP = 0 .618) in this same analysis, pointing to receiver-cell specificity in the GABA-B receptor-mediated taurine signaling axis: CD4 + T cells are not causal targets of NK cell SLC6A6-mediated GABBR1 signaling at the population level, whereas B cells are. This observation echoes the direction-selectivity previously noted for SLC6A6 ŌĆōGABBR1 in the B cells ŌåÆ CD4 + T cells 71 direction (PIP = 0 .54), where B cells rather than NK cells were the active sender 8,9 .The single-discovery result here contrasts with the four discoveries identified in the reverse direction (CD4 + T cells ŌåÆ NK cells), underscoring a directional asymmetry in which CD4 +

T helper cells are more potent causal communicators to NK cells than NK cells are to CD4 +

T cells at the population level in peripheral blood. 72 0.54 

PIP = 0.5

ReceptorŌłÆmodulated ligand effects: NK cells ŌłÆ> CD4 + T cells (MRŌłÆCCC) Figure S41: Receptor-modulated effect curves ( ╦å╬▓X + ╦å╬▓XZ ┬Ę Z/ SD( Z)) for the NK cells ŌåÆ CD4 + T cells analysis. Only the single discovery pair (PIP > 0.5) is displayed in the Adhesion by ICAM panel. The ICAM1 ŌĆōITGAL curve crosses zero essentially at the population-mean ITGAL level and descends to negative values at above-average LFA-1 expression, consistent with the near-purely interaction-driven suppressive signal. 75 S2.4.3 NK Cells ŌåÆ CD8 + T Cells 

Across 830 donors, MR-CCC evaluated 42 ligandŌĆōreceptorŌĆōpathway triplets for the NK cell (sender) to CD8 + T cell (receiver) direction and identified two high-confidence causal com-munication signals with PIP exceeding 0.5: ICAM1 ŌĆōITGAL within the Adhesion by ICAM pathway (PIP = 0 .862) and CXCL8 ŌĆōCXCR2 within the Chemokine signaling pathway (PIP = 0 .546) (Figures S42ŌĆōS44). The dominant discovery, ICAM1 ŌĆōITGAL (PIP = 0 .862, ╦å╬▓X = 1 .46, ╦å╬▓XZ = ŌłÆ8.36), implicates NK cell ICAM-1 as a causal regulator of CD8 + T cell Adhesion pathway activ-ity through LFA-1 (encoded by ITGAL ), with an interaction magnitude that is the sec-ond largest of any discovered triplet in the entire analysis 20,23 . The large positive main effect and strongly negative interaction produce a sign-reversing effect curve that crosses zero approximately 0 .18 standard deviations above the mean ITGAL level. CD8 + T cells with below-average LFA-1 expression experience a strongly stimulatory response to NK cell ICAM-1 engagement; above this threshold, the effect reverses sharply, and CD8 + T cells with high LFA-1 expression undergo a steeply amplified suppression of Adhesion pathway activity that grows in magnitude with receptor density. Because LFA-1 is progressively upregulated during CD8 + T cell activation and effector differentiation 23 , this pattern suggests that NK cell ICAM-1 preferentially suppresses activated and effector-like CD8 + T cells while leaving naive or resting cells with low LFA-1 expression either unaffected or mildly stimulatedŌĆöa receptor-gated regulatory mechanism consistent with the established capacity of NK cells to selectively eliminate or restrain over-activated T cells. The ICAM1 ŌĆōITGAL triplet has now been discovered across all three non-B cell receiver types in the NK sender directionsŌĆöNK cells ŌåÆ B cells (PIP = 0 .782, ╦å╬▓XZ = ŌłÆ2.13), NK cells ŌåÆ CD4 + T cells (PIP = 0 .54, ╦å╬▓XZ = ŌłÆ0.910), and here with the largest PIP and by far the largest interaction magnitude ( ╦å╬▓XZ = ŌłÆ8.36). The progressive increase in interaction magnitude across receiver cell types (CD4: ŌłÆ0.910; B: ŌłÆ2.13; CD8: ŌłÆ8.36) indicates that the NK cell ICAM-1ŌĆōLFA-1 suppressive axis is most potently amplified in CD8 + T cells, consistent with their higher constitutive and activation-induced LFA-1 expression relative to B and CD4 + T cells 20,23 .76 The second discovered triplet, CXCL8 ŌĆōCXCR2 (PIP = 0 .546, ╦å╬▓X = 0 .443, ╦å╬▓XZ = 0 .530), identifies NK cell-derived CXCL8 (IL-8) as a causal activator of CD8 + T cell Chemokine pathway activity through the CXCR2 receptor. Both the main effect and the interaction are positive, placing the zero crossing at approximately ŌłÆ0.84 standard deviations below the mean CXCR2 expression level, outside the bulk of the observed distribution. The causal effect is therefore positive across essentially all observed CD8 + T cells and grows with receptor density: CD8 + T cells expressing higher levels of CXCR2 show a progressively amplified Chemokine pathway response to NK cell CXCL8 production. CXCL8 is produced by NK cells upon activation and engages CXCR2 on effector and terminally differentiated CD8 + Tcell subsets, which express CXCR2 at higher levels than naive or central memory cells 31 . The positive interaction is consistent with a feed-forward chemokine amplification mechanism in which NK-derived CXCL8 increasingly activates Chemokine pathway gene expression in CD8 + T cells that are already in a chemokine-responsive, high-CXCR2 state. Notably, 

CXCL8 ŌĆōCXCR2 was the highest-ranking sub-threshold triplet in the CD8 + T cells ŌåÆ CD4 +

T cells direction (PIP = 0 .367), where it did not achieve discovery strength; here the same triplet is discovered from the NK sender direction, indicating that NK cells rather than CD8 + T cells are the dominant population-level source of CXCL8 driving CXCR2-mediated signaling in CD8 + T cells in this cohort. Among sub-threshold triplets, ICAM4 ŌĆōITGAL (PIP = 0 .476, ╦å╬▓X = 0 .159, ╦å╬▓XZ = ŌłÆ1.55) was the highest-ranking near-miss; the positive main effect and negative interaction produce a sign-reversing curve crossing zero near +0 .10 standard deviations above the mean ITGAL 

level, with the majority of CD8 + T cells falling in the suppressive regime. Its near-discovery alongside the confirmed ICAM1 ŌĆōITGAL signal suggests that NK cell ICAM4 contributes a partially consistent suppressive adhesion contact that falls just below the discovery threshold. 

ICAM1 ŌĆōITGB2 (PIP = 0 .398) and ICAM1 ŌĆōITGAM (PIP = 0 .369) represent additional sub-threshold ICAM pairs, both consistent with broad NKŌĆōCD8 adhesive contacts that do not individually achieve the consistency threshold at the population level 23 .

IL18 ŌĆōIL18R1 (PIP = 0 .376) was the highest-ranking Interleukin near-miss; this triplet was discovered in the CD8 + T cells ŌåÆ Monocytes direction (PIP = 0 .82), where CD8 + T77 cells were the sender, but here NK cells as sender to CD8 + T cells fall below the threshold, suggesting that the IL-18ŌĆōIL-18R1 axis from NK cells to CD8 cells is insufficiently consistent at the population level compared with the CD8-to-monocyte direction 32 .

IFNG ŌĆōIFNGR1 (PIP = 0 .029) and IFNG ŌĆōIFNGR2 (PIP = 0 .039) both received near-zero support, consistent with the pattern observed across all NK sender directions: despite NK cells being a major source of IFN-╬│, the NK cell cis-eQTL-driven variation in IFNG 

expression does not produce a detectable causal signal on CD8 + T cell Interferon pathway activity at the population level 10,28 .78 0.86 0.55

The NK cells ŌåÆ monocytes direction (8 discoveries spanning GABA, interferon, interleukin, and prostaglandin signaling, n = 651 donors) is presented in full detail in the Real Data Analysis section of the main manuscript and is therefore omitted here. 

S2.5 Monocytes as Sender 

S2.5.1 Monocytes ŌåÆ B Cells 

Across 665 donors, MR-CCC evaluated 41 candidate ligandŌĆōreceptorŌĆōpathway triplets for the Monocyte (sender) to B cell (receiver) direction and identified eight high-confidence causal communication signals with PIP exceeding 0.5, spanning three pathway classes: five Adhesion by ICAM pairs ( ICAM1 ŌĆōITGAM , PIP = 0 .780; ICAM1 ŌĆōITGAL , PIP = 0 .732; 

ICAM1 ŌĆōITGB2 , PIP = 0 .721; ICAM1 ŌĆōITGAX , PIP = 0 .628; ICAM4 ŌĆōITGAL , PIP = 0.548), two Signaling by Interleukin triplets ( IL1B ŌĆōIL1RAP , PIP = 0 .685; IL15 ŌĆōIL2RB ,PIP = 0 .548), and one Signaling by Prostaglandin triplet ( AKR1C3 ŌĆōPTGDR , PIP = 0 .687) (Figures S45ŌĆōS47). 

Adhesion by ICAM signals. The five discovered ICAMŌĆōintegrin triplets constitute the densest single-ligand adhesion discovery cluster in the Monocyte sender directions: all four evaluated ICAM1 ŌĆōintegrin pairs are simultaneously discovered, joined by ICAM4 ŌĆō

ITGAL 20,23 . Despite sharing the same ligand, the four ICAM1 pairs divide into two quali-tatively distinct groups based on the sign of the interaction term. 

ICAM1 ŌĆōITGAL (PIP = 0 .732, ╦å╬▓X = 0 .613, ╦å╬▓XZ = 2 .36) and ICAM1 ŌĆōITGAX (PIP = 0 .628, ╦å╬▓X = 0 .955, ╦å╬▓XZ = 0 .320) both show positive main effects and positive inter-actions, yielding monotonically stimulatory effect curves across the observed receptor ex-pression range. For ICAM1 ŌĆōITGAL the zero crossing lies at approximately 0 .26 standard deviations below the mean ITGAL level, meaning the stimulatory effect is active across essen-tially all B cells and grows steeply with LFA-1 density. For ICAM1 ŌĆōITGAX the interaction is smaller and the zero crossing lies near ŌłÆ3.0 standard deviations below the mean, making this effectively a pure positive main effect that uniformly stimulates the Adhesion pathway 82 of CD11c-expressing B cells. 

ICAM1 ŌĆōITGAM (PIP = 0 .780, ╦å╬▓X = 1 .13, ╦å╬▓XZ = ŌłÆ2.17), ICAM1 ŌĆōITGB2 (PIP = 0 .721, ╦å╬▓X = 1 .05, ╦å╬▓XZ = ŌłÆ1.38), and ICAM4 ŌĆōITGAL (PIP = 0 .548, ╦å╬▓X = 0 .617, ╦å╬▓XZ = ŌłÆ1.15) form the second group: large positive main effects combined with negative interactions yield sign-reversing curves that cross zero at +0 .52, +0 .76, and +0 .54 standard deviations above their respective receptor means. B cells expressing Mac-1 ( ITGAM ), ╬▓2

(ITGB2 ), or LFA-1 ( ITGAL , via ICAM4) below these thresholds experience net stimula-tion; those above them transition to progressively stronger suppression of Adhesion pathway activity 20,21 .The most striking cross-direction contrast concerns ICAM1 ŌĆōITGAL : in every NK cell sender direction in which this triplet was discovered, the interaction was large and negative 

(NK cells ŌåÆ B cells: ╦å╬▓XZ = ŌłÆ2.13; NK cells ŌåÆ CD4 + T cells: ╦å╬▓XZ = ŌłÆ0.910; NK cells 

ŌåÆ CD8 + T cells: ╦å╬▓XZ = ŌłÆ8.36), yielding receptor-gated suppression of Adhesion pathway activity at high LFA-1. From the monocyte sender, the same triplet yields a large positive 

interaction ( ╦å╬▓XZ = +2 .36), converting the curve from receptor-amplified suppression to receptor-amplified stimulation. This sender-specific sign reversal of the interaction term for the identical ligandŌĆōreceptorŌĆōpathway triplet illustrates the capacity of MR-CCC to detect qualitatively opposite causal consequences of the same molecular contact depending on the cellular source of the ligand. 

Signaling by Interleukin. IL1B ŌĆōIL1RAP (PIP = 0 .685, ╦å╬▓X = 0 .462, ╦å╬▓XZ = ŌłÆ0.098) identifies monocyte-derived IL-1 ╬▓ as a causal activator of B cell Interleukin pathway activity through the IL-1 receptor accessory protein 29 . Monocytes are the primary cellular source of IL-1 ╬▓ in peripheral blood, and B cells express functional IL-1 receptor complexes that regulate B cell activation and antibody production. The negligibly small interaction term places the zero crossing at approximately +4 .7 standard deviations above the mean IL1RAP 

level, far outside the observed data range; this triplet is therefore a near-purely main-effect discovery in which monocyte IL-1 ╬▓ exerts a uniformly positive stimulatory effect on B cell Interleukin pathway activity that is essentially independent of IL-1RAP expression level. 

IL15 ŌĆōIL2RB (PIP = 0 .548, ╦å╬▓X = 0 .453, ╦å╬▓XZ = ŌłÆ2.11) implicates monocyte-derived 83 IL-15 as a causal regulator of B cell Interleukin pathway activity through the shared IL-2R ╬▓

chain (encoded by IL2RB ; CD122) 3,4 . Monocytes constitutively express IL-15R ╬▒ (IL15RA )and transpresent IL-15 to neighboring cells, making them a biologically plausible cellular source for this signal. The positive main effect and large negative interaction yield a sign-reversing curve that crosses zero at approximately +0 .22 standard deviations above the mean IL2RB level: B cells with below-average IL-2R ╬▓ expression experience net stimula-tion, while those above the thresholdŌĆöassociated with a more activated or memory B cell phenotypeŌĆöundergo progressively stronger suppression, consistent with receptor-mediated negative feedback under high IL-2R ╬▓ expression. This triplet was previously discovered in the B cells ŌåÆ CD8 + T cells direction (PIP = 0 .518), where B cells were the sender; its discovery here from the monocyte sender direction indicates that the IL-15ŌĆōIL-2R ╬▓ axis to B cells is activated by multiple cellular sources in peripheral blood. 

Signaling by Prostaglandin. AKR1C3 ŌĆōPTGDR (PIP = 0 .687, ╦å╬▓X = ŌłÆ0.225, ╦å╬▓XZ =

ŌłÆ1.85) identifies monocyte aldo-keto reductase 1C3 ( AKR1C3 ) as a causal suppressor of B cell Prostaglandin pathway activity through the prostaglandin D 2 receptor (DP1, encoded by PTGDR ). AKR1C3 is a multifunctional lipid-metabolizing enzyme expressed at high levels in monocytes that catalyses the synthesis of prostaglandin F 2╬▒ and related eicosanoids from prostaglandin H 2, and can interconvert prostaglandin D 2 metabolites that engage the DP1 receptor on lymphocytes 35,36 . Both the main effect and the interaction are negative, with the zero crossing at approximately 0 .12 standard deviations below the mean PTGDR 

expression levelŌĆöessentially at the population mean. Monocytes with higher AKR1C3-mediated eicosanoid synthesis activity therefore exert an increasingly strong suppression of B cell Prostaglandin DP1 pathway activity, with the suppression uniformly experienced by essentially all B cells expressing PTGDR at or above the mean. This is the first direction in the analysis in which AKR1C3 ŌĆōPTGDR is discovered; it was a sub-threshold near-miss (PIP = 0 .365) in the NK cells ŌåÆ Monocytes direction. Several triplets narrowly missed the discovery threshold. ITGB1 ŌĆōADGRE5 (PIP = 0.492) was the highest-ranking sub-threshold triplet and a borderline near-miss; this triplet was among the top discoveries in the CD4 + T cells ŌåÆ B cells direction (PIP = 0 .992) and was 84 also discovered in the CD4 + T cells ŌåÆ Monocytes direction (PIP = 0 .597), but monocyte 

╬▓1 integrin-to-B cell CD97 signaling falls just below the discovery threshold here. ICAM4 ŌĆō

ITGB2 (PIP = 0 .482) was also a close near-miss within the Adhesion by ICAM cluster. 

IFNG ŌĆōIFNGR2 (PIP = 0 .468) was the highest-ranking non-ICAM, non-prostaglandin sub-threshold triplet; monocytes can produce low levels of IFN-╬│ under activation conditions, but the population-averaged signal does not achieve discovery strength, consistent with IFN-╬│

being a more characteristic product of T and NK cells 10 .85 0.73 0.72 0.78 0.63 0.55 0.55 0.69 0.69 

PIP = 0.5

In the Signaling by Prostaglandin panel, AKR1C3 ŌĆōPTGDR crosses zero just below the population mean and descends steeply to strongly negative values at high 

PTGDR expression. 88 S2.5.2 Monocytes ŌåÆ CD4 + T Cells 

Across 691 donors, MR-CCC evaluated 42 ligandŌĆōreceptorŌĆōpathway triplets for the Mono-cyte (sender) to CD4 + T cell (receiver) direction and identified three high-confidence causal communication signals with PIP exceeding 0.5: IL15 ŌĆōIL15RA and IL15 ŌĆōIL2RB within the Signaling by Interleukin pathway (PIP = 0 .711 and PIP = 0 .694, respectively) and 

SEMA4D ŌĆōCD72 within the Signaling by Semaphorin pathway (PIP = 0 .674) (Figures S48ŌĆō S50). The two IL-15 discoveries jointly implicate monocyte-derived IL-15 as a causal com-municator to CD4 + T cells through two distinct receptor chains of the IL-15/IL-2 receptor complex. Monocytes constitutively express IL15RA and transpresent IL-15 to neighbor-ing lymphocytes in trans 2,4 , making them a primary cellular vehicle for IL-15 delivery in peripheral blood. 

IL15 ŌĆōIL15RA (PIP = 0 .711, ╦å╬▓X = 0 .381, ╦å╬▓XZ = ŌłÆ0.898) has a positive main effect and a negative interaction, yielding a sign-reversing curve that crosses zero at approximately 0.42 standard deviations above the mean IL15RA level. CD4 + T cells with below-average IL-15R ╬▒ expression experience net stimulation of Interleukin pathway activity by monocyte IL-15, while those with high IL15RA expression undergo progressively stronger attenuation and eventual suppression, consistent with receptor saturation or negative feedback at high transpresentation receptor densities. This same triplet was the dominant discovery in the B cells ŌåÆ CD4 + T cells direction (PIP = 0 .867), but with the opposite interaction sign ( ╦å╬▓XZ =+2 .28), producing a monotonically stimulatory curve. The sender-specific sign reversal of the IL15RA interaction termŌĆöpositive from B cell sender, negative from monocyte senderŌĆö indicates that the same IL-15R ╬▒-mediated transpresentation interface produces qualitatively different receptor-modulated outcomes in CD4 + T cells depending on the cellular source, consistent with structural differences in the B cell versus monocyte IL-15 transpresentation complex affecting the downstream signaling outcome 3,4 .

IL15 ŌĆōIL2RB (PIP = 0 .694, ╦å╬▓X = ŌłÆ0.348, ╦å╬▓XZ = 1 .33) exhibits the opposite sign struc-ture: a negative main effect and a large positive interaction. The zero crossing lies at ap-proximately 0 .26 standard deviations above the mean IL2RB expression level. CD4 + T cells with below-average IL-2R ╬▓ expression experience net suppression of Interleukin pathway 89 activity in response to monocyte IL-15, while those expressing IL2RB above this thresh-old experience progressively amplified stimulation. The opposing main-effect signs of the two co-discovered IL-15 tripletsŌĆöpositive main effect through IL15RA , negative main effect through IL2RB ŌĆöindicate that the two receptor chains impose qualitatively different baseline responses to monocyte IL-15, with the IL-2R ╬▓ chain acting as a gatekeeper that converts a baseline-suppressive signal into a stimulatory one only in CD4 + T cells that express it at sufficient levels. 

SEMA4D ŌĆōCD72 (PIP = 0 .674, ╦å╬▓X = 0 .192, ╦å╬▓XZ = 2 .61) identifies monocyte-expressed SEMA4D (CD100) as a causal activator of CD4 + T cell Semaphorin pathway activity through CD72. The near-zero main effect and large positive interaction place the zero crossing at approximately 0 .07 standard deviations below the mean CD72 levelŌĆöessentially at the pop-ulation mean. The causal signal is therefore almost entirely interaction-driven and operates across the full observed CD4 + T cell population: CD4 + T cells expressing CD72 at or above the mean experience a steeply increasing stimulation of Semaphorin pathway activity as monocyte SEMA4D production rises. CD72 was first characterized as a counter-receptor for SEMA4D (CD100) on B cells, where CD100ŌĆōCD72 signaling modulates B cell activa-tion thresholds and humoral immunity 37 ; its discovery here as a receptor on CD4 + T cells for monocyte-derived CD100 signals extends this semaphorin axis to a myeloidŌĆōT helper cell communication context, consistent with the broader role of SEMA4D in lymphocyte co-stimulation and cytoskeletal regulation 27 .Several triplets narrowly missed the discovery threshold. Both ITGAV ŌĆōADGRE2 (PIP = 0 .469, ╦å╬▓X = ŌłÆ0.240, ╦å╬▓XZ = ŌłÆ0.577) and ITGAV ŌĆōADGRE5 (PIP = 0 .436, ╦å╬▓X = ŌłÆ0.200, ╦å╬▓XZ = ŌłÆ0.369) were notable Integrin pathway near-misses; both exhibit negative main effects and negative interactions, producing monotonically suppressive curves across the observed receptor expression range. The ADGRE2 and ADGRE5 receptors (EMR2 and CD97) were discovered from CD4 + T cell senders in the CD4 + T cells ŌåÆ NK cells direction (PIP = 0 .910 and PIP = 0 .858, respectively) but fall below the discovery threshold here, suggesting that the integrinŌĆōadhesion-GPCR axis between these cell types is directionally asymmetric: more consistently detected from CD4 + T cell sender to NK receiver than from monocyte sender 90 to CD4 + T cell receiver at the population level 19,24 . SEMA4D ŌĆōPLXNB2 (PIP = 0 .358) was the highest-ranking sub-threshold Semaphorin triplet beyond the discovered SEMA4D ŌĆō

CD72 , consistent with monocyte SEMA4D engaging multiple receptor systems on CD4 +

T cells but only the CD72-mediated axis achieving discovery strength. CLEC2B ŌĆōKLRF1 

(PIP = 0 .304) and IL18 ŌĆōIL18RAP (PIP = 0 .336) both fell below threshold; the latter was discovered from NK cell senders to monocytes (PIP = 0 .976), again reflecting the directional specificity of IL-18 receptor signaling in this cohort 32,33 .

IFNG ŌĆōIFNGR1 (PIP = 0 .039) and IFNG ŌĆōIFNGR2 (PIP = 0 .031) both received near-zero PIPs, consistent with monocytes not being a dominant physiological source of IFN-╬│ in peripheral blood 10 .91 0.71 0.69 0.67 

PIP = 0.5

ReceptorŌłÆmodulated ligand effects: Monocytes ŌłÆ> CD4 + T cells (MRŌłÆCCC) Figure S50: Receptor-modulated effect curves ( ╦å╬▓X + ╦å╬▓XZ ┬Ę Z/ SD( Z)) for the Mono-cytes ŌåÆ CD4 + T cells analysis. ascends from negative to positive, crossing zero at +0 .26 SD above the mean; the two curves form an X-shaped crossing pair with opposite slopes despite sharing the same ligand. In the Signaling by Semaphorin panel, SEMA4D ŌĆōCD72 passes near zero just below the population mean and rises steeply to strongly positive values at high CD72 expression. 94 S2.5.3 Monocytes ŌåÆ CD8 + T Cells 

Across 678 donors, MR-CCC evaluated 42 ligandŌĆōreceptorŌĆōpathway triplets for the Monocyte (sender) to CD8 + T cell (receiver) direction and identified three high-confidence causal com-munication signals with PIP exceeding 0.5: ICAM1 ŌĆōITGAL and ICAM1 ŌĆōITGAX within the Adhesion by ICAM pathway (PIP = 0 .654 and PIP = 0 .598, respectively) and IL1B ŌĆō

IL1RAP within the Signaling by Interleukin pathway (PIP = 0 .549) (Figures S51ŌĆōS53). The two discovered ICAM pairs both engage monocyte ICAM-1 as ligand but through different integrin receptors on CD8 + T cells, producing qualitatively opposite interaction-modulated outcomes 20,23 . ICAM1 ŌĆōITGAL (PIP = 0 .654, ╦å╬▓X = 0 .541, ╦å╬▓XZ = ŌłÆ3.02) has a positive main effect and a large negative interaction, yielding a sign-reversing curve that crosses zero at approximately 0 .18 standard deviations above the mean ITGAL level. CD8 +

T cells with LFA-1 expression below this threshold experience net stimulation of Adhesion pathway activity by monocyte ICAM-1 engagement; those above it transition to progressively stronger suppression, with the majority of the observed CD8 + T cell population falling in the suppressive regime given the near-mean zero crossing. This suppressive pattern from monocyte sender to CD8 + T cell receiver is consistent with the NK cell sender directions, where ICAM1 ŌĆōITGAL carried uniformly negative interactions (NK cells ŌåÆ CD8 + T cells: ╦å╬▓XZ = ŌłÆ8.36). Strikingly, however, the same triplet from the same monocyte sender to B cell receiver showed the opposite sign ( ╦å╬▓XZ = +2 .36, Monocytes ŌåÆ B cells), converting receptor-amplified suppression in CD8 + T cells into receptor-amplified stimulation in B cells. The receiver-specific sign reversal of the ICAM1ŌĆōLFA-1 interaction term between CD8 + Tcell and B cell targets from the identical monocyte sender underscores the cell-type specificity of adhesion-mediated causal communication detected by MR-CCC. 

ICAM1 ŌĆōITGAX (PIP = 0 .598, ╦å╬▓X = 0 .468, ╦å╬▓XZ = 1 .49) has a positive main effect and a positive interaction, yielding a monotonically increasing effect curve with a zero crossing at approximately 0 .31 standard deviations below the mean ITGAX expression level. Monocyte ICAM-1 therefore exerts a broadly stimulatory causal effect on the Adhesion pathway activity of CD8 + T cells expressing CD11c (encoded by ITGAX ), with the stimulation growing in magnitude at higher CD11c densities 21 . This positive interaction from monocyte ICAM-1 95 through CD11c is consistent with the same triplet in the Monocytes ŌåÆ B cells direction ( ╦å╬▓XZ = +0 .32), where CD11c-expressing B cells were similarly stimulated. The shared positive interaction sign for ICAM1 ŌĆōITGAX across B cell and CD8 + T cell receiversŌĆöin contrast to the opposing ICAM1 ŌĆōITGAL signsŌĆöindicates that the integrin ╬▒ chain identity (╬▒X vs ╬▒L) is the key determinant of whether monocyte ICAM-1 contact is stimulatory or suppressive in the receiver cell. 

IL1B ŌĆōIL1RAP (PIP = 0 .549, ╦å╬▓X = 0 .231, ╦å╬▓XZ = ŌłÆ0.392) identifies monocyte-derived IL-1 ╬▓ as a causal activator of CD8 + T cell Interleukin pathway activity through the IL-1 receptor accessory protein 29 . The positive main effect and moderate negative interaction yield a sign-reversing curve that crosses zero at approximately 0 .59 standard deviations above the mean IL1RAP level. CD8 + T cells with below-average or moderately above-average IL-1RAP expression experience net stimulation by monocyte IL-1 ╬▓; those with the highest IL-1RAP expression undergo progressive attenuation and reversal, consistent with receptor-mediated negative feedback under high accessory protein density. This triplet was also discovered from monocyte sender to B cell receiver (PIP = 0 .685, ╦å╬▓XZ = ŌłÆ0.098), but there the interaction was negligibly small and the effect was essentially a uniform pos-itive main effect; the more pronounced negative interaction here ( ╦å╬▓XZ = ŌłÆ0.392) indicates that IL-1RAP-mediated attenuation of monocyte IL-1 ╬▓ signaling is a more receptor-density-dependent process in CD8 + T cells than in B cells. Among sub-threshold triplets, ICAM3 ŌĆōITGAL (PIP = 0 .429, ╦å╬▓X = ŌłÆ0.192, ╦å╬▓XZ = 1 .83) was the highest-ranking near-miss; the negative main effect and large positive interaction produce a sign-reversing curve that crosses zero at approximately 0 .10 standard deviations above the mean ITGAL level, with CD8 + T cells expressing LFA-1 above the mean ex-periencing increasing stimulation of Adhesion pathway activity by monocyte ICAM3. Its near-discovery alongside the confirmed ICAM1 ŌĆōITGAL signal highlights the complex het-erogeneity of monocyte ICAM-family contacts at the monocyteŌĆōCD8 + T cell interface. IL15 ŌĆō

IL2RB (PIP = 0 .482) and IL15 ŌĆōIL15RA (PIP = 0 .431) were the highest-ranking Interleukin near-misses; both IL-15 pairs were discovered from monocyte sender to CD4 + T cell receiver (PIPs = 0 .694 and 0 .711, respectively), but fall below the discovery threshold here, suggest-96 ing that the monocyte IL-15 transpresentation axis targets CD4 + T cells more consistently than CD8 + T cells at the population level in this cohort 3,4 .

IFNG ŌĆōIFNGR1 (PIP = 0 .166) received a higher PIP than in most sender directions but still fell well below the discovery threshold; monocytes are not a dominant physiological source of IFN-╬│, and the moderate PIP here likely reflects partial overlap of the monocyte 

IFNG cis-eQTL with IFN-╬│-responsive CD8 + T cell pathway activity at the population level 10,28 .97 0.65 0.60 0.55

ReceptorŌłÆmodulated ligand effects: Monocytes ŌłÆ> CD8 + T cells (MRŌłÆCCC) Figure S53: Receptor-modulated effect curves ( ╦å╬▓X + ╦å╬▓XZ ┬Ę Z/ SD( Z)) for the Mono-cytes ŌåÆ CD8 + T cells analysis. Only the three discovery pairs (PIP > 0.5) are displayed, grouped into the two pathway panels with confirmed discoveries (Adhesion by ICAM and Sig-naling by Interleukin). In the Adhesion by ICAM panel, ICAM1 ŌĆōITGAL descends steeply from positive to negative, crossing zero near +0 .18 SD above the mean, while ICAM1 ŌĆō

ITGAX rises monotonically, remaining positive across the majority of the observed CD11c expression range with a zero crossing near ŌłÆ0.31 SD below the mean; the two curves form a crossing pair reflecting the divergent interaction signs for the ╬▒L versus ╬▒X integrin chains. In the Signaling by Interleukin panel, the IL1B ŌĆōIL1RAP curve is positive at low to moderate 

IL1RAP expression and crosses zero near +0 .59 SD above the mean. 100 S2.5.4 Monocytes ŌåÆ NK Cells 

Across 651 donors, MR-CCC evaluated 41 ligandŌĆōreceptorŌĆōpathway triplets for the Mono-cyte (sender) to NK cell (receiver) direction and identified one high-confidence causal com-munication signal with PIP exceeding 0.5: CXCL8 ŌĆōCXCR2 within the Chemokine signaling pathway (PIP = 0 .518) (Figures S54ŌĆōS56). The sole discovery, CXCL8 ŌĆōCXCR2 (PIP = 0 .518, ╦å╬▓X = 0 .375, ╦å╬▓XZ = ŌłÆ0.180), iden-tifies monocyte-derived CXCL8 (IL-8) as a causal activator of NK cell Chemokine pathway activity through the CXCR2 receptor. Monocytes are among the most prolific cellular sources of CXCL8 in peripheral blood, and NK cells express CXCR2 on cytotoxic and terminally dif-ferentiated subsets 31 . The positive main effect and negligibly small negative interaction term place the zero crossing at approximately +2 .08 standard deviations above the mean CXCR2 

expression levelŌĆöfar above the bulk of the observed NK cell distribution. The causal effect is therefore positive across essentially the full observed CXCR2 expression range, with only the most extreme high-CXCR2 NK cells approaching neutral or mildly negative territory. This triplet is a near-pure main-effect discovery: monocyte CXCL8 production exerts a broadly uniform stimulatory effect on NK cell Chemokine pathway activity that is largely independent of receptor expression level. CXCL8 ŌĆōCXCR2 was also discovered in the NK cells ŌåÆ CD8 + T cells direction (PIP = 0 .546), where NK cells were the sender; its appearance here from the monocyte sender direction confirms that CXCL8ŌĆōCXCR2 signaling is an active chemokine communication axis in both directions involving NK cells, with monocytes and NK cells each capable of driving CXCR2-mediated pathway activity in the other cell type. The overall sparsity of discoveries in this directionŌĆöa single borderline triplet, in con-trast to the eight discoveries identified in the reverse direction (NK cells ŌåÆ Monocytes)ŌĆö represents the strongest directional asymmetry in the entire analysis. NK cells act as potent causal communicators to monocytes via IFN-╬│, IL-18, IL-1 ╬▓, prostaglandin, and GABA receptor axes, while monocytes return only a minimal consistent causal footprint on NK cell pathway activity at the population level. This asymmetry is consistent with the estab-lished immunological relationship between NK cells and monocytes in peripheral blood: NK 101 cells provide activation, licensing, and cytokine signals to monocytes, while monocyte-to-NK communication in resting peripheral blood is more limited and dominated by contact-independent chemokine cues 10,18 .Several triplets narrowly missed the discovery threshold. IL1B ŌĆōIL1RAP (PIP = 0 .471, ╦å╬▓X = 0 .328, ╦å╬▓XZ = 0 .389) was the highest-ranking near-miss; both coefficients are posi-tive, producing a monotonically stimulatory curve with a zero crossing near ŌłÆ0.84 standard deviations below the mean IL1RAP level. This near-discovery is noteworthy because IL1B ŌĆō

IL1RAP was confirmed from monocyte senders to both B cells (PIP = 0 .685) and CD8 +

T cells (PIP = 0 .549), and was also discovered from NK cell senders to monocytes (PIP = 0 .716); its sub-threshold PIP here suggests that monocyte IL-1 ╬▓ signaling to NK cells through IL-1RAP is less consistent at the population level than to lymphocyte targets 29 .

SLC6A6 ŌĆōGABBR1 (PIP = 0 .442, ╦å╬▓X = ŌłÆ0.235, ╦å╬▓XZ = 0 .422) was also a notable near-miss; the negative main effect and positive interaction produce a sign-reversing curve crossing zero near +0 .56 standard deviations above the mean GABBR1 level, with NK cells expressing high GABBR1 showing a net stimulatory response to monocyte SLC6A6 taurine-transport activity. This contrasts with the NK cell sender directions (NK cells ŌåÆ B cells and NK cells ŌåÆ Monocytes), where SLC6A6 ŌĆōGABBR1 carried large negative interactions produc-ing receptor-gated suppression; the positive interaction here from monocyte sender to NK receiver is opposite in sign, but falls below the discovery threshold 8,9 . ICAM1 ŌĆōITGAX (PIP = 0 .393) was the highest-ranking Adhesion by ICAM near-miss, consistent with the mono-cyte ICAM1ŌĆōCD11c axis that was discovered targeting both B cells and CD8 + T cells but does not achieve consistency to NK cells at the population level. 

IFNG ŌĆōIFNGR1 (PIP = 0 .076) and IFNG ŌĆōIFNGR2 (PIP = 0 .162) both received low support, consistent with monocytes not being a dominant physiological source of IFN-╬│ 10 .All Semaphorin, Integrin, Cholesterol, WNT, and Thromboxane pathway triplets received PIPs below 0.35. 102 0.52

ReceptorŌłÆmodulated ligand effects: Monocytes ŌłÆ> NK cells (MRŌłÆCCC) Figure S56: Receptor-modulated effect curves ( ╦å╬▓X + ╦å╬▓XZ ┬Ę Z/ SD( Z)) for the Mono-cytes ŌåÆ NK cells analysis. Only the single discovery pair (PIP > 0.5) is displayed in the Signaling by Chemokines panel. The CXCL8 ŌĆōCXCR2 curve is nearly flat and positive across the bulk of the observed CXCR2 expression range, with a zero crossing near +2 .08 standard deviations above the mean, consistent with a near-pure main-effect discovery. 105 Across all 19 supplementary ordered pairs, MR-CCC consistently assigns high poste-rior probability to biologically established signaling axes while returning near-zero PIPs for mechanistically implausible directions. Recurrent triplets such as ICAM1 ŌĆōITGAL , PT-GES3 ŌĆōPTGER2 , and SLC6A6 ŌĆōGABBR1 appear across multiple senderŌĆōreceiver combina-tions with interaction signs that are specific to the sender cell type and receiver cell type, illustrating that MR-CCC detects directionally and cellularly resolved causal signals rather than co-expressed pairs that would be flagged indiscriminately under association-based meth-ods. The directional asymmetries observedŌĆömost strikingly the eight discoveries from NK cells to monocytes versus the single borderline discovery in the reverse directionŌĆöare consis-tent with known immunological communication hierarchies in peripheral blood and reinforce the biological validity of the causal inference framework established in the main manuscript.
